    &lt;details class="details-overlay details-reset"&gt;

  <summary>

<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="    &lt;div id=&quot;readme&quot; class=&quot;Box-body readme blob js-code-block-container p-5 p-xl-6 gist-border-0&quot;&gt;
&lt;article class=&quot;markdown-body entry-content container-lg&quot; itemprop=&quot;text&quot;&gt;&lt;h1 dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;user-content-linux-netspeed&quot; class=&quot;anchor&quot; aria-hidden=&quot;true&quot; href=&quot;#linux-netspeed&quot;&gt;&lt;svg class=&quot;octicon octicon-link&quot; viewBox=&quot;0 0 16 16&quot; version=&quot;1.1&quot; width=&quot;16&quot; height=&quot;16&quot; aria-hidden=&quot;true&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill-rule=&quot;evenodd&quot; d=&quot;M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;&lt;/a&gt;Linux-NetSpeed&lt;/h1&gt;"><pre class="notranslate"><code class="notranslate">    &lt;div id="readme" class="Box-body readme blob js-code-block-container p-5 p-xl-6 gist-border-0"&gt;
&lt;article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"&gt;&lt;h1 dir="auto"&gt;&lt;a id="user-content-linux-netspeed" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#linux-netspeed"&gt;&lt;svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"&gt;&lt;path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;&lt;/a&gt;Linux-NetSpeed&lt;/h1&gt;
</code></pre></div>
<div dir="auto">https://git.io/JYxKU" &amp;&amp; chmod +x tcpx.sh &amp;&amp; ./tcpx.sh
卸载内核版本
wget -O tcp.sh "<a href="https://git.io/coolspeeda" rel="nofollow">https://git.io/coolspeeda</a>" &amp;&amp; chmod +x tcp.sh &amp;&amp; ./tcp.sh<p dir="auto"></p>
<p dir="auto">关联action自动编译内核
<a href="https://github.com/ylx2016/kernel/">https://github.com/ylx2016/kernel/</a></p>
<p dir="auto">双持bbr+锐速
bbr 添加
echo "net.core.default_qdisc=fq" &gt;&gt; /etc/sysctl.d/99-sysctl.conf
echo "net.ipv4.tcp_congestion_control=bbr" &gt;&gt; /etc/sysctl.d/99-sysctl.conf
sysctl -p</p>
<p dir="auto">编辑锐速文件
nano /appex/etc/config</p>
<p dir="auto">检测代码有BUG，如果锐速正常 运行查看
bash /appex/bin/lotServer.sh status | grep "LotServer"</p>
<p dir="auto">检查bbr 内核默认bbr算法不会有输出
lsmod | grep bbr</p>
<p dir="auto">检查centos安装内核
grubby --info=ALL|awk -F= '$1=="kernel" {print i++ " : " $2}'</p>
<p dir="auto">查看当前支持TCP算法
cat /proc/sys/net/ipv4/tcp_allowed_congestion_control
查看当前运行的算法
cat /proc/sys/net/ipv4/tcp_congestion_control
查看当前队列算法
sysctl net.core.default_qdisc</p>
<p dir="auto">命令： uname -a
作用： 查看系统内核版本号及系统名称</p>
<p dir="auto">命令： cat /proc/version
作用： 查看目录"/proc"下version的信息，也可以得到当前系统的内核版本号及系统名称</p>
<p dir="auto">真实队列查看？ 更改队列算法可能需要重启生效
tc -s qdisc show</p>
<p dir="auto">/etc/sysctl.d/99-sysctl.conf
sysctl --system</p>
<p dir="auto">ylx2016与chiakge、cx9208无任何关系
bbsplus算法原作者
<a href="https://blog.csdn.net/dog250/article/details/80629551" rel="nofollow">https://blog.csdn.net/dog250/article/details/80629551</a>

<a href="https://github.com/cx9208/bbrplus">https://github.com/cx9208/bbrplus</a>
新版bbrplus
<a href="https://github.com/UJX6N/bbrplus-5.10">https://github.com/UJX6N/bbrplus-5.10</a>
xanmod官网
<a href="https://xanmod.org" rel="nofollow">https://xanmod.org</a>
Zen官网
<a href="https://liquorix.net/" rel="nofollow">https://liquorix.net/</a>
锐速
<a href="https://moeclub.org/2017/03/09/14/" rel="nofollow">https://moeclub.org/2017/03/09/14/</a>
其他内核
<a href="https://github.com/alibaba/cloud-kernel">https://github.com/alibaba/cloud-kernel</a>
<a href="https://github.com/Tencent/TencentOS-kernel">https://github.com/Tencent/TencentOS-kernel</a>
官方编译好的内核
<a href="https://sourceforge.net/projects/xanmod/files/releases/current" rel="nofollow">https://sourceforge.net/projects/xanmod/files/releases/current</a>
<a href="https://elrepo.org/linux/kernel/el7/x86_64/RPMS/" rel="nofollow">https://elrepo.org/linux/kernel/el7/x86_64/RPMS/</a>

<a href="https://mirrors.tencent.com/tlinux/2.4/tlinux/x86_64/RPMS/" rel="nofollow">https://mirrors.tencent.com/tlinux/2.4/tlinux/x86_64/RPMS/</a>
<a href="https://bintray.com/multipath-tcp/mptcp_rpm/mptcp/v0.95.1#files" rel="nofollow">https://bintray.com/multipath-tcp/mptcp_rpm/mptcp/v0.95.1#files</a>
